[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing session triggered a critical security exception indicating a file [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath traversal vulnerability during archive extraction. The issue occurs in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander` example utility of the Apache Commons Compress library, where an [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted file’s path escapes the intended output directory. The exception is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraised by the `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer, classifying this as a [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzerSecurityIssueCritical.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer input caused [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto be thrown. The sanitizer detected that one or more archive entries, when [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpanded, would write to a path outside the designated output directory [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp8274279934669413339/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a path traversal vulnerability: untrusted archive entries can specify [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelative paths [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “..[0m[35m/../etc/[0m[95mpasswd[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or absolute paths to escape the target [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction directory.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePathTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:346[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which enforces that resolved[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths remain within a base directory.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer’s `checkPath` and `copyMismatchMvHook` methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m293[0m[39m and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intercept suspicious file operations before the actual I/O occurs.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows multiple overloads of `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m216[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m336[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m[1;36m52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdrives the entry point and is not the root cause.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m523[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Critical Logic[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The specialized `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overload bypasses the safe `resolveIn`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath resolution used elsewhere, instead performing manual `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`startsWith` checks and then using a custom `createParentDirectory` that follows [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting filesystem symlinks.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Attackers can first introduce a symlink entry pointing outside the extraction [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot, and then subsequent file entries end up being written through that [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlink—evading the simple `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check and escaping the intended directory.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must preserve:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Support for symlink entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUnix symlinks in ZIP[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • File‐and‐directory extraction features of the example.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No changes to harness/fuzzing logic.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy Overview[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unify path resolution by reusing the safe `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich does `[0m[1;35mparent.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + `startsWith` guard[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the manual resolution logic.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Harden symlink handling:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Normalize and strictly validate both the symlink’s path *and* its target [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst the extraction root before creating any symlink.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Do *not* follow existing symlinks when creating parent directories of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meither symlink or regular files—use `Files.createDirectories` on the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` directly.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor bypass[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m the old `createParentDirectory` invocation in this [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverload, as it may follow attacker-controlled symlinks. Use [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Files.createDirectories` instead.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For regular [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon-symlink, non-directory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m entries, after calling `resolveIn`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimply ensure the parent directories exist, then copy the entry’s contents via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstreams.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In `Org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.java`, locate the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        public void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile archive, Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      and inside its loop over `ZipArchiveEntry` entries:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Symlink Branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreplace lines ~[0m[1;36m476[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Compute the link path safely:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path linkPath = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mlinkPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip: "[0m[39m + targetDirectory + [0m[32m" + "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[32m" -> "[0m[39m + linkPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Read the symlink target name, then resolve + validate:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          String rawTargetName = [0m[1;35mIOUtils.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUTF_8[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path symlinkTarget = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawTargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35msymlinkTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Symlink target outside extraction root: "[0m[39m + [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrawTargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Create only the immediate parent of the link—do *not* follow any existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlinks:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path linkParent = [0m[1;35mlinkPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinkParent != null && ![0m[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinkParent[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinkParent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Finally, if the link doesn’t already exist, create it:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinkPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mFiles.createSymbolicLink[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinkPath, symlinkTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Regular‐File Branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreplace lines ~[0m[1;36m490[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m500[0m[39m and remove [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`createParentDirectory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Obtain a safe target with the common guard:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Ensure its parent directories are created without following symlinks:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path parent = [0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent != null && ![0m[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Copy entry contents via streams:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35marchive.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mzae[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               OutputStream os = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mIOUtils.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, os[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Deprecate or leave `createParentDirectory` unused in this overload; other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgeneric expand methods remain unchanged.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Works[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By leveraging `resolveIn`, we get a robust defense against “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mabsolute‐path based escapes before any filesystem operations occur.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Symlink creation is now subject to the same “stay within the root” checks, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious symlinks pointing outside are rejected upfront.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing follow‐symlink behavior in directory creation kills the attacker’s [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mability to hijack later writes via a symlink planted earlier.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to harness or fuzzing logic; existing example [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and tests should continue to pass for benign archives.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archives relying on nested symlinks resolving outside the root [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma less common [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse case[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now fail with an `IOException`. This is acceptable: the example [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility should not allow such unsafe behavior.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The removed `createParentDirectory` logic may have handled some edge‐case [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory sequences differently; if necessary, reuse its simple “mkdirs” logic [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout following symlinks.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify via existing tests and add a unit test confirming that symlinks [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargetting outside the extraction directory are rejected.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During fuzzing, the sanitizer `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` flagged a ZIP [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack trace pinpointed the problem to `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen handling ZIP archive entries.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No assumptions were made about the root cause; the report simply records that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzzer found an unhandled path-traversal case in the archive expander.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises before any call to helper methods like [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`createParentDirectory`, i.e., during initial path resolution.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both file entries and Unix symlink entries must be guarded against names [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or absolute paths.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing code normalized the path for file entries but did not [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistently normalize or restrict symlink targets.  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `Expander.java` around the loop over `ZipArchiveEntry` instances:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Replaced direct calls to `IOUtils.toString` for symlink targets with [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo-stage normalization:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – Compute `linkPath = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – Enforce `[0m[1;35mlinkPath.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or throw `IOException`  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Read the raw link target name as UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, normalize it against [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetDirectory` into `symlinkTarget`, and enforce the same prefix check.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Create missing parent directories for the link and then create the symlink [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly if it does not already exist.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • For non-directory, non-symlink entries:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – Introduced a helper call `[0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpresumably to [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – Create missing parent directories, then copy entry data via [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOUtils.copy`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Kept the original `createParentDirectory` method but removed some of its [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mearlier uses in favor of the new directory-creation logic.[0m                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:96[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m105[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipArchiveEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mnextEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.isUnixSymlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Locate and fix the syntax error**  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect `Expander.java` around line [0m[1;36m509[0m[39m: the `createParentDirectory` helper is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing its closing brace [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing the “illegal start of expression” at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompile time.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add the necessary `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` immediately after the `return current;` line to properly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclose the method. Verify that all other braces in the `while [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;35mentries.hasMoreElements[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` and `if/else if` blocks are balanced.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unify and harden path‐normalization logic**  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the ad‐hoc symlink‐branch resolution with the same `resolveIn` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mresolve + normalize + prefix check[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m used by the generic `expand<T>` [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation. Concretely:  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. For the link itself, call `Path linkPath = [0m[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of manual `resolve` + `normalize` + `startsWith`.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. For the symlink target, mimic `resolveIn` semantics by resolving the raw [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget name against the extraction root, normalizing, and enforcing [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before proceeding.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach removes duplication, ensures any “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” in the entry name or the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymlink target is caught, and adheres to the existing, battle‐tested code pattern.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Simplify directory‐creation**  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminate the specialized `createParentDirectory` call in the ZIP‐specific [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode. Instead, after obtaining `linkPath` or `targetPath`, do:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path parent = [0m[1;35mpath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent != null && ![0m[1;35mFiles.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This matches the generic `expand<T>` behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m83[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and reduces [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplexity.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `createParentDirectory` is no longer referenced anywhere, consider removing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit; otherwise, ensure it’s properly closed and hardened as described below.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Harden or retire `createParentDirectory`**  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If retaining the helper for other branches, insert a `current = [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcurrent.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` inside its loop and after following symlinks, then assert `if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcurrent.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Directory traversal detected"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore creating each directory.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents malicious symlinks in the path from escaping the extraction [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **End‐to‐end validations**  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recompile and run the existing test suite to confirm no regressions.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the Jazzer fuzz target [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Expander.expand`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure the original File [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath Traversal is now blocked for both file entries and symlink entries.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that the harness and other archive formats [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTar, 7z, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still work [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas before.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Justification**  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fixing the missing brace restores syntax correctness without changing surrounding[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using `resolveIn` guarantees consistent normalization + prefix checks, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the asymmetric treatment of symlinks.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Simplifying directory creation aligns ZIP handling with the proven generic [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation, reducing code duplication and the risk of subtle traversal bugs.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Hardening or removing `createParentDirectory` ensures that no unchecked symlink [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan escape the root directory during directory‐creation.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy preserves existing behavior for non‐malicious archives, enforces [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistent security checks, resolves the compile error, and integrates seamlessly [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the initial codebase without touching harnesses, tests, or external [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                 at                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0mExpander.jav[1;92ma:216[0m[1m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                 at [1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mExpanderFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:52[0m[1m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: 7bb3f9683ba8f59b                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue is a security sanitizer alert [1m([0mFuzzerSecurityIssueCritical[1m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         triggered by a file path traversal in `Expander.expand` when processing ZIP entries [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mincluding symlinks[1m)[0m. A patch was attempted to add explicit path normalization and  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         root‐directory checks for both file extraction and symlink creation, replace manual [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         byte‐copy with `IOUtils.copy`, and simplify parent‐directory creation. After        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         applying the patch, the build fails with several Java compilation errors in         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.java`, citing “illegal start of expression” and “class, interface, or     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         enum expected” at and around the modified lines.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - When fuzzing the Apache Commons Compress `Expander` example, Jazzer’s          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         FilePathTraversal sanitizer flagged a critical security issue: a ZIP entry’s name   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         could escape the intended extraction root [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/.../output/q/[0m[95mr[0m`[1m)[0m via a crafted     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         filename.                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace shows `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` being invoked during the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `copyMismatchMvHook` call in the `expand` method of `Expander.java`.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The issue arises during processing of both regular entries and Unix‐style      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         symlink entries [1m([0m`[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The sanitizer identifies that either the path of the extracted file or the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         target of a created symlink resolves outside the intended root directory.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Both extraction routines [1m([0mfor files and for symlinks[1m)[0m lacked a uniform         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “normalize and verify prefix” pattern.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the `if [1m([0m[1;35mzae.isUnixSymlink[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m` branch:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Introduced `linkPath = [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and a check that `[1;35mlinkPath.startsWith[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory[1m)[0m`, throwing an `IOException`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         on violation.                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Read the raw target via UTF-[1;36m8[0m, normalized `symlinkTarget =                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1m([0mrawTargetName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, and checked it against the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         target root.                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Ensured parent directories exist [1m([0m`Files.createDirectories`[1m)[0m and created the [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         symlink only if it didn’t already exist.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the regular‐entry branch [1m([0m`else if [1m([0m![1;35mzae.isDirectory[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m:                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Replaced manual `Path` adjustments with a hypothetical                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory[1m)[0m` method [1m([0mnot present in original code[1m)[0m.             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Ensured parent directories exist, then copied data by opening an             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `OutputStream` via `Files.newOutputStream` and calling `IOUtils.copy`.              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Removed the original `createParentDirectory` invocations inside those          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         branches; left the helper method at the bottom.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Patch Application & Build Log                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - After patching `Expander.java`, a Maven compile step runs and reports six      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         errors in `Expander.java`:                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • `[1m[[0m[1;36m509[0m,[1;36m5[0m[1m][0m illegal start of expression`                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Multiple “class, interface, or enum expected” at lines [1;36m528[0m, [1;36m531[0m, [1;36m533[0m, [1;36m535[0m.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The errors indicate that the Java source is syntactically invalid—likely due   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to mismatched braces or stray statements [1m([0mfor example, the added code closed the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `expand` method too early or introduced statements outside any method or class[1m)[0m.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The build terminates with “BUILD FAILURE” before any further testing or        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         security checks can run.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. Areas for Further Investigation                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The `expand` method in `Expander.java` around lines [1;36m475[0m–[1;36m540[0m: verify that all   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         added `if/else` blocks and their braces correctly nest within the method.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The use of `[1;35mzae.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mtargetDirectory[1m)[0m`: this method does not exist in the [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         public API—investigate the intended replacement for manual `resolve` + `normalize`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logic.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Correct placement of the closing brace for `createParentDirectory` versus the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         class-level closing brace—ensure the helper remains inside the class and not        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         inadvertently nested or truncated.                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Reconcile the removal of the original `createParentDirectory` calls with the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         helper’s actual invocation sites.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Review imports and any missing dependency on `IOUtils.copy` and                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Files.newOutputStream` to confirm no missing statics or unchecked exceptions.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify imports at the top of `Expander.java`:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.ArchiveEntry;`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.zip.ZipArchiveEntry;`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import java.nio.file.Files;`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import java.nio.file.Path;`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `import org.apache.commons.io.IOUtils;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor reading symlink targets[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   These imports already exist; no new imports are required.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Rationale:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By shifting to `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`, we eliminate manual normalization [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmistakes and zip‐slip vulnerabilities in one call.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inlining the entire symlink and file logic in the `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod removes the incorrect dependencies on non‐existent methods and removes the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomplex `createParentDirectory` logic that was not needed for ZIP entries.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This preserves the helper `createParentDirectory` for other archive formats [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., Tar[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, ensures proper directory‐and‐class brace structure, and resolves the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“illegal start of expression” errors by restoring correct Java syntax.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. After applying these changes, rebuild the Maven project. The syntax errors [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maround lines [0m[1;36m509[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m536[0m[39m should disappear, and the security sanitizer tests will [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to enforce path traversal checks via the fuzzer harness as before. [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
